319a6(1): bu gsum gyi phye/ byi la'i bar chad re dang sbyar/ ma sbyar na yang nyes pa med/ tshogs par bsten nas bza' bar bya/ re re bsten yang nyes pa med/ dam rdzas sman du bsgyur te bsten
319a7(1): pa'i cho ga rdzogs s+ho// nad med sems kyi byang chub grub rtags bshad pa'o//  gas kyang kyim mabyud kyi nag pa bzhugs// dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po la phyag 'tshal
319a8(1): lo/ de nas yang dag bshad bya ba/ bcom ldan nyid kyi sku gsung thugs/ rdo rje rnams las byung ba yi/ rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po yis// lho phyogs rgya mtsho bar rgal nas// de na gshin
